Introduction

This document provides an overview of the spatial BLUE wth the multi-spectral drone imagery data, agronomic and malting quality data. The goal is to conduct the first BLUE stage with the vegetation indices and explore data distribution.

3. Fit simple BLUE model for spec

envs    <-  unique(data_sp$Env)
traits <- colnames(data_sp)[c(8:10, 12:17)]
raw_dat <- data_sp                                  
## -------------------------------------------------------------
##  containers
## -------------------------------------------------------------
fit_list  <- list()   
pred_list <- list()   
data$GID<- as.character(data$GID)
timepoints <- unique(data$Timepoint)
## -----------------------------------------------------------------
##  loops
## -----------------------------------------------------------------
for (tr in traits) {

  fits_vi <- list()

  for (e in envs) {
    
    dat_sub <- raw_dat %>%
      filter(Env == e, !is.na(.data[[tr]])) %>%
      mutate(
        GID = factor(GID),
        Row = factor(Row),
        Col = factor(Column)
      )
    
    timepoints <- unique(dat_sub$Timepoint)

    for (tp in timepoints) {
      dat_sub1 <- dat_sub %>% filter(Timepoint == tp)

      ## model -----------------------------------------------------------------
      mod <- tryCatch(
        asreml(
          fixed    = reformulate("GID", response = tr),
          random   = ~ar1(Row):ar1(Column),
          residual = ~ units,
          data     = dat_sub1
        ),
        error = function(err) {
          message("asreml failed for ", tr, " | ", e, " | tp ", tp,
                  " : ", err$message)
          NULL
        }
      )

      ## store fit -------------------------------------------------------------
      fits_vi[[paste(e, tp, sep = "_")]] <- mod

      ## predictions -----------------------------------------------------------
      if (!is.null(mod)) {
        pred_result <- tryCatch({
          pred <- predict(mod, classify = "GID")$pvals %>%
            as_tibble() %>%
            transmute(
              VI        = tr,
              Env       = e,
              Timepoint = tp,
              GID,
              Predicted = predicted.value,
              SE        = std.error
            )

          pred_list[[length(pred_list) + 1]] <- pred
        }, error = function(err) {
          message("Prediction failed for ", tr, " | ", e, " | tp ", tp,
                  " : ", err$message)
          NULL
        })
      }
    } # time‑point loop
  }   # environment loop

  fit_list[[tr]] <- fits_vi
}     # trait loop

5. Fit simple BLUE model for ag

envs    <- unique(data_ag$Env)
traits <- colnames(data_ag)[c(9:12)]
raw_dat <- data <-  data_ag                                   

## -------------------------------------------------------------
fit_list  <- list()
pred_list <- list() 
data$GID<- as.character(data$GID)
## -----------------------------------------------------------------
for (tr in traits) {

  fits_vi <- list()

  for (e in envs) {
    
          dat_sub <- raw_dat %>%
        filter(Env == e,
               !is.na(.data[[tr]])) %>%
        mutate(
          GID = factor(GID),
          Row = factor(Row),
          Col = factor(Column)
        )

      ## model -----------------------------------------------------------------
      mod <- tryCatch(
        asreml(
          fixed    = reformulate("GID", response = tr),   #
          random   = ~Row + ~Column,
          residual = ~ units,              
          data     = dat_sub
        ),
        error = function(err) {
          message("asreml failed for ", tr, " | ", e,
                  " : ", err$message)
          NULL
        }
      )

      ## store fit -------------------------------------------------------------
      fits_vi[[paste(e,  sep = "_")]] <- mod

      ## predictions -----------------------------------------------------------
      if (!is.null(mod)) {
        pred <- predict(mod,
                        classify = "GID")$pvals %>%
          as_tibble() %>%
          transmute(
            VI          = tr,
            Env = e,
            GID,
            Predicted   = predicted.value,
            SE          = std.error
          )

        pred_list[[length(pred_list) + 1]] <- pred
      }
  }   # environment loop

  fit_list[[tr]] <- fits_vi
}     # trait loop

6. Fit simple BLUP model for MQ

envs    <- c("MCG23","HELF24")
traits <- colnames(data_mq)[8:21]
data_mq<- left_join(data_mq, data_ag[,c(2,5,6)], by= "plot_id")
raw_dat <- data <-  data_mq %>% na.omit() %>% droplevels()

## -------------------------------------------------------------
fit_list  <- list()   
pred_list <- list()
data$GID<- as.character(data$GID)

## -----------------------------------------------------------------

for (tr in traits) {

  fits_vi <- list()

  for (e in envs) {
    
          dat_sub <- raw_dat %>%
        filter(Env == e) %>%
        mutate(
          GID = factor(GID),
          Row = factor(Row),
          Col = factor(Column)
        )

      ## model -----------------------------------------------------------------
      mod <- tryCatch(
        asreml(
          fixed    = reformulate("1", response = tr),   #  ~ 1
          random   = ~GID + ~ar1(Row):ar1(Column),                             # genotype effect
          residual = ~ units,               # spatial correction
          data     = dat_sub
        ),
        error = function(err) {
          message("asreml failed for ", tr, " | ", e,
                  " : ", err$message)
          NULL
        }
      )

      ## store fit -------------------------------------------------------------
      fits_vi[[paste(e,  sep = "_")]] <- mod

      ## predictions -----------------------------------------------------------
      if (!is.null(mod)) {
  pred <- tryCatch({
    predict(mod, classify = "GID")$pvals %>%
      as_tibble() %>%
      transmute(
        VI        = tr,
        Env       = e,
        GID,
        Predicted = predicted.value,
        SE        = std.error
      )
  },
  error = function(err) {
    message("asreml predict failed for ", tr, " | ", e,
            " : ", err$message)
    NULL
  })

  if (!is.null(pred)) {
    pred_list[[length(pred_list) + 1]] <- pred
  }
}
  }   # environment loop

  fit_list[[tr]] <- fits_vi
}     # trait loop

VImats <- list()
multi<- preds_m
VIs <- unique(multi$VI)

VImats <- list()

tibble [96,740 × 6] (S3: tbl_df/tbl/data.frame)

 - attr(*, "heading")= chr "- The predictions are obtained by averaging across the hypertable\n  calculated from model terms constructed so"| __truncated__
multi <- multi %>% filter(!VI == "GDVI") 
# Step 1: Make the dataframe wider so each VI is a column
multi_wide <- multi[,1:5] %>%
  pivot_wider(
    names_from = VI,
    values_from = Predicted
  )

VImats <- list()

for (e in unique(multi_wide$Env)) {
  VImats[[e]] <- list()
  for (i in VIs) {
    subdata <- multi_wide[multi_wide$Env == e, c("Timepoint", i, "GID")]
    wide_df <- tidyr::pivot_wider(
      data        = subdata,
      names_from  = Timepoint,
      values_from = i
    )
    VImats[[e]][[i]] <- wide_df
  }
}

wide_list <- multi_wide %>%
  group_split(Env) %>%
  set_names(unique(multi_wide$Env)) %>%
  map(~ pivot_wider(.x,
                    id_cols = GID,
                    names_from = Timepoint,
                    values_from = c(NDVI, NDRE, EVI, GNDVI, NRI, SAVI, ENDVI, GIPVI, PSRI),
                    names_glue = "{.value}_TP{Timepoint}"
  ))


VImats$MCG25[["combined"]]<- wide_list$MCG25
VImats$HELF24[["combined"]]<- wide_list$HELF24
VImats$MCG23[["combined"]]<- wide_list$MCG23
VImats$SNY22[["combined"]]<- wide_list$SNY22
VImats$KET21[["combined"]]<- wide_list$KET21
save(VImats, file= "data/VImatBLUE.Rdata")
